However, later previews speculated how was it impossible for Solid Snake to be in the game's settings, leading to the conclusion it was a young incarnation of his father.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>116<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>117<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>118<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> A comparison between Solid Snake's and Big Boss's characters was made by <i>IGN</i> in an article titled "Stars Thunderdome: Snake vs. Big Boss."<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>119<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The character's appearance in <i>Metal Gear Solid 4</i> has received mostly positive opinions. Before it was released, various speculations were made regarding his role. As he was the only one who suffered from a drastic change in appearance, <i>IGN</i> commented that the most famous rumor was the one of his body deteriorating across the game.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>120<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Moreover, since it had been announced it would be his last appearance, <i>IGN</i> and <i>GamesRadar</i> wondered whether the character would die during the game and if Raiden would replace him following his death.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>121<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>122<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <i>GamesRadar</i> commented that his character was one of the few gaming characters that aged across video games.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>123<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <i>GamePro</i> also listed Old Snake as one of the biggest surprises from the game, as the character was found interesting in contrast to pessimistic thoughts they had before the game's release.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>124<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/GameDaily" title="GameDaily">GameDaily</a></i> listed the "old hero" as one of their list of top video game archetypes, using the old version of the character as an example of this.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>125<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Play_(UK_magazine)" title="Play (UK magazine)">PLAY</a></i> gave praise to his moustache considering how highly detailed it is, and represents the change from Solid Snake's character.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>126<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> On the other hand, <i>1UP.com</i> criticized it as the most gracelessly aging characters as it gave negative messages about aging.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>127<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <i>1UP.com</i> listed their fight as the 13 "most dumbass" boss battles for its simple style in comparison to other more challenging bosses from <i>Metal Gear Solid 3</i> and its excessive length for a hand-to-hand fight between two old people.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>128<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The design resulted in mixed reactions regarding whether or not the character kept his original sex appeal.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>129<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>130<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p><i><a href="/wiki/GameDaily" title="GameDaily">GameDaily</a></i> made Solid Snake top their <a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros." title="Super Smash Bros."><i>Smash Bros.</i></a> characters list,<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>131<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> while <i>PLAY</i> listed him as one of the characters they wanted to be playable in <i><a href="/wiki/Mortal_Kombat_(2011_video_game)" title="Mortal Kombat (2011 video game)">Mortal Kombat</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>132<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The character customization in <i><a href="/wiki/Soulcalibur_IV" title="Soulcalibur IV">Soulcalibur IV</a></i> that allowed to create Solid Snake was listed by <i>UGO</i> as one of the best ones from the series owing to his popularity within gamers.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>133<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Gavin Jasper of <i><a href="/wiki/Den_of_Geek" title="Den of Geek">Den of Geek</a></i> ranked Solid Snake as 12th of <i>Super Smash Bros. Ultimate</i> characters, and stated that "bringing Snake in <i>Smash Bros.</i> was an act of pure dominance."<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>134<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Jeremy Parish of <i><a href="/wiki/Polygon_(website)" title="Polygon (website)">Polygon</a></i> ranked 73 fighters from <i><a href="/wiki/Super_Smash_Bros._Ultimate" title="Super Smash Bros. Ultimate">Super Smash Bros. Ultimate</a></i> "from garbage to glorious", listing Solid Snake as 18th, stating that "The legendary super-soldier Solid Snake remains one of gaming's greatest and most tragic figures."<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>135<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> People expressed some disappointment on <i>Super Smash Bros. Ultimate</i> when Solid Snake wears a skintight stealth suit, and the rendition being completely changed. Leaving the character's butt being reduced.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>136<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Akio Otsuka's and David Hayter's performances as Solid Snake's voice actors has received praise. Ōtsuka remembers being surprised during his debut as a result of the large amount of dialogue Solid Snake was given.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>137<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Hayter's performance was called one of the greatest in gaming as well as one of the character's most recognizable traits.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>138<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>139<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2013, <i><a href="/wiki/Game_Informer" title="Game Informer">Game Informer</a></i> ranked Hayter's role as Solid Snake as the seventh most memorable character voice in video games for "a portrayal that's considered to be a real classic in the history of video game voice acting".<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>140<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2024, a poll conducted by <a href="/wiki/British_Academy_of_Film_and_Television_Arts" title="British Academy of Film and Television Arts">BAFTA</a> with around 4,000 respondents named Solid Snake as the fourteenth most iconic video-game character of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>141<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Controversy">Controversy</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Solid_Snake&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Controversy"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>In the <i><a href="/wiki/Tekken_7" title="Tekken 7">Tekken 7</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Evo_2019" title="Evo 2019">Evo 2019</a> finals, the character was used to have a chat with developer <a href="/wiki/Katsuhiro_Harada" title="Katsuhiro Harada">Katsuhiro Harada</a>. The organizers of Evo stated this was a joke as many fans believed it was a hint for a possible usage of the character as downloadable content.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>142<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> David Hayter complained about this joke as Evo did not consult Konami or him when using the audio.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>143<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p>
